Question #182 (ID: 481035)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 1st Paper | Years: 2024, 2022, 2017, 2016 | Boards: Barisal Board, Barisal Board, Dinajpur Board, Barisal Board | Tags: Barisal Board, Barisal Board, Dinajpur Board, Barisal Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
A future plan of life helps one to reach one's goal. A student must have a definite future plan in life. Now, write a dialogue between you and your friend Rahim/Rahima about your future plan of life.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
Monir : Hello, Rahim!

Rahim : Hi, Nayeem! Where're are you going?

Monir : I'm going to my cousin to know something about MBBS.

Rahim : MBBS! Are you interested to study MBBS in future?

Monir : Yes, I'm.

Rahim : Why have you chosen it?

Monir : Because, I want to be a doctor.

Rahim : Why are you so passionate about it?

Monir : For two reasons. It's a noble profession as it provides me with the opportunity of serving the helpless patients. And another one is, it is a prestigious profession. What about you, Karim?

Rahim : My aim is different. I want to study ELT. ELT means English Language Teaching. I want to have an MA in ELT from the Institute of Modern Languages under Dhaka University.

Monir : Why have you chosen that?

Rahim : I want to teach English at different levels. I want to raise the standard and. quality of English in Bangladesh. Developing four skills of language learning among our students is my mission.

Monir : It's wonderful!

Rahim : Yes. It's essential for human resource development.

Monir : I wish you for your future plan.

Rahim : Thanks a lot and I wish you would be able to fulfil your aim.

Monir : Thank you and bye.

Word Meaning: interested (adj) – আগ্রহী; passionate (adj) আবেগপ্রবণ; noble (adj) - মহৎ; prestigious (adj) -মর্যাদাপূর্ণ; aim (n) – লক্ষ্য; mission (v) – জীবনেরব্রত; essential (adj) – প্রয়োজনীয়; wish (v) – শুভকামনা করা।

Explanation:
এই উত্তর সঠিক কারণ সংলাপে ছাত্রটি তার ভবিষ্যৎ লক্ষ্য, কেন তা চায় এবং সেই লক্ষ্য অর্জনের জন্য করণীয় ধাপগুলো স্পষ্টভাবে ব্যক্ত করে, যা পরিকল্পনা এবং উৎসাহ তৈরিতে সাহায্য করে। এতে ছাত্র ও পাঠক উভয়ই বুঝতে পারে কোন বিষয় শেখা, কোন দক্ষতা অর্জন এবং কীভাবে সময় ও পরিশ্রম বিনিয়োগ করলে লক্ষ্যে পৌঁছানো যাবে।

Question #183 (ID: 481036)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 1st Paper | Years: 2024, 2016 | Boards: Sylhet Board, Dinajpur Board | Tags: Sylhet Board, Dinajpur Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Suppose, you are Nabil/Nabila. You read in Blue Bird School, Sylhet. Now, write a dialogue between you and the librarian of your school about borrowing a book.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
Nabila : Good afternoon, Sir

Librarian : Good afternoon. How can I help you?

Nabila : I want to borrow Bangladesh and Global Studies book. What should I do for this?

Librarian : Well. Do you have the library card?

Nabila : Yes, Sir.

Librarian : Then you've to submit the card here to borrow the book. We'll preserve your card until you return the book.

Nabila : Ok. How many days can I keep the book?

Librarian : Oh! it's only three days. Please remember, you have to take care of the book. You'll be fully responsible if any damage occurs to the book or it is lost.

Nabila : Ok. Don't worry, Sir. I'll take care of it.

Librarian : Please, write your name, class and put a signature în the register. Thank you.

Nabila : You're welcome.

Word Meaning: borrow (v) – ধার করা; submit (v) – জমা দেওয়া; responsible (adj) – দায়ী; damage (n) – ক্ষতি; register (n) – নিবন্ধন খাতা।

Explanation:
এই ডায়alogটি সঠিক কারণ এতে লাইব্রেরিয়ানের সাথে বই ধার নেওয়ার সব প্রয়োজনীয় অংশ রয়েছে — শুভেচ্ছা, বইয়ের নাম ও লেখকের তথ্য, ধার নেওয়ার উদ্দেশ্য ও প্রত্যাবর্তনের সময় নিয়ে আলোচনা এবং ধন্যবাদ জানা। এটি শিক্ষার্থীদের ভদ্রভাবে অনুরোধ করা এবং স্পষ্টভাবে তথ্য দেওয়ার মাধ্যমে ধার নেওয়ার নিয়মবদ্ধ প্রক্রিয়া বুঝতে সাহায্য করে।

Question #184 (ID: 481031)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 1st Paper | Years: 2020 | Boards: Dinajpur Board | Tags: Dinajpur Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Mr. Rahman is a retired officer. Usually, he goes for a walk everyday early in the morning. One day while he was walking in the morning, he saw a man lying senseless by the side of the road. He went nearer to the man …......

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:


Explanation:
The correct answer is right because when someone is found senseless the natural and responsible action is to approach and assess their condition to see if they are conscious or need help. This reflects basic emergency response: safely check for responsiveness and breathing, then call for help or give first aid as needed.

Question:
Once a schoolboy named Talha was returning from school. On the way to his home, he saw a boy of his age. The boy was working in a workshop. His body was covered with dirt, oil and other chemicals. Talha became curious about the boy. He asked the boy………

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:


Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা: যে উত্তরটি সঠিক তা বলছে যে শিশুটি পরিবারকে সাহায্য করার জন্য কাজ করছে এবং তাই স্কুলে যায় না, কারণ তার বিয়ে-আচরণ ও ময়লা-তেলের অবস্থান থেকে দেখা যায় সে কর্মজীবী এবং দারিদ্র্যজনিত কারণে স্কুল ছেড়েছে। এটি শিশু শ্রম ও দারিদ্র্যের সামাজিক কারণ তুলে ধরে, এবং বোঝায় কেন শিক্ষার সুযোগ ও পরিবারিক সমর্থন গুরুত্বপূর্ণ।

Question #186 (ID: 480982)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 1st Paper | Years: 2024, 2018 | Boards:  | Tags: Cumilla Board, All Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Read the beginning of a story below. Add at least ten sentences to complete the story and give a suitable title of it.

Rafi is a worker of a big factory in Dhaka. There are more than 500 workers in the factory. One day while he was working, a loud sound was heard. Fire! Fire! Help! Help!..........................

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
[math]~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~[/math] Look before You LeapRafi is a worker of a big factory in Dhaka. There are more than 500 workers in the factory. One day while he was working, a loud sound was heard. Fire! Fire! Help! Help! As ill news runs apace, the news spread very fast among the workers. But no one noticed whether there was actually any fire or not. Having just heard the news, without any confirmation, all the workers of the factory became desperate to come outside.But the factory had only one exit and the path which led to this gate was very narrow. Even three men or women could not pass through this path side by side at a time. So, when all the workers of the factory were trying to come out along this narrow path, the path became congested with the workers. Many workers feli down on the path because of the jostling in the crowd and were trampled by other workers. Some of them received severe injuries. In a word, a chaotic situation had been prevailing in the factory. After observing the situation, the authority of the factory took steps to pacify the workers. The authority announced through loud speaker that the news was a rumour and no fire had broken out. Actually, a pipe containing colour had burst out in the dying section but it caused no casualties. After hearing this announcement twice, the workers understood their follies and went back to their work.Word Meaning: ill news (phr) - খারাপ সংবাদ; runs apace (phr) - দ্রুত ছড়ানো; confirmation (n) - নিশ্চিতকরণ; desperate (adj) – মরিয়া; exit (n) - প্রস্থান; narrow (adj) - সর; congested (adj) -জনাকীর্ণ; jostle (v) ধাজ্ঞাধাজি কর trample (v) - পদদলিত করা; chaotic situation (phr) - বিশৃঙ্খল অবস্থা; pacify (v) - শান্ত করা; announce (v) - যোবলা দেওয়া; rumour (n) – গুজব; burst out (v)- বিস্ফোরিত হওয়া; casualty (n) - ক্ষয়ক্ষতি/দুর্ঘটনা।

Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা: গল্পের সম্পূরক অংশে আগুনের ধ্বংস ঠেকাতে কর্মীদের দ্রুত উদ্ধারের দৃশ্য, দমকলের আগমন ও নিরাপত্তা পরিচর্যার নির্দেশনা দেখানো হয়েছে, তাই শিরোনামটি ঘটনাটির মূল উপজীব্য—অগ্নি দুর্ঘটনা ও সঙ্কট মোকাবিলা—প্রতিফলিত করে। এই উত্তরটি সঠিক কারণ এটি ঘটনার ধারাবাহিকতা ধরে রেখে করণীয় (শান্ত থাকা, জরুরি পথ ব্যবহার, দলগত সহযোগিতা) ও পারিপার্শ্বিক ফলাফল (আহত কম হওয়া, শিক্ষা গ্রহণ) স্পষ্টভাবে তুলে ধরে। সরল ভাষা ও বিশিষ্ট ঘটনাবলি ছাত্রদের দ্রুত বুঝতে এবং নৈতিক শিক্ষা আয়ত্তে সাহায্য করে।

Question #187 (ID: 480983)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 1st Paper | Years: 2020, 2020, 2019, 2017, 2016, 2012, 2012, 2012, 2011, 2010, 2010 | Boards: Rajshahi Board, Sylhet Board, Barisal Board, Sylhet Board, Chittagong Board, Chittagong Board, Barisal Board, Rajshahi Board, Dhaka Board | Tags: Rajshahi Board, Sylhet Board, Barisal Board, Sylhet Board, Chattogram Board, Chattogram Board, Barisal Board, Cumilla Board, Jessore Board, Rajshahi Board, Dhaka Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
One day a crow became very thirsty. He flew from one place to another in search of water. But he found no water. He continued his search for water............

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
Completed story with meaning:

One day à crow became very thirsty. He flew from one place to another in search of water. But be found no water. He continued his search for water in order to save his life. At last he saw a jar at a distance and flew down to it. There was a little water at the bottom of the jar but it was too low for the crow. The crow tried to upset the jar but he was not strong enough to do it. The crow was in a fix what to do. But he did not lose heart. He tried to overtum the jar but failed. He was about to fly away when he saw some stones a little away from the jar. At once he hit upon a plan. He picked up the stones one by one and dropped them into the jar. When he dropped a large number of stones, the water in the jar rose high enough for him to reach it. Then the crow quenched its thirst drinking water to his heart's content.

Selected Vocabulary (নির্বাচিত শব্দার্থ): One day-একদিন। crow-কাক, thirsty-তৃষ্ণার্ত, পিপাসার্ক in search of-c continue-চালিয়ে যাওয়া। in order to-উদ্দেশ্যে। save-রক্ষা করা; at last-অবশেষে, শেষে। jar-কলস; at a distance at the bottom-তলদেশে: low-নি: upset- উল্টানো, strong-শক্তিশালী, enough-যথেষ্ট। fail-বার্থ হওয়া। fly away-উড়ে যাওয়া: stone-পাথর। little away-একটু দূরে। at once-তৎক্ষণাৎ hit upon a plan-পরিকল্পনা করা, বুদ্ধি আটা, pick up-উঠানো, drop-ফেলা a large number of -বহু সংখ্যক; enough-যথেষ্ট। reach-পৌছানো। quench-নিবারণ করা, মেটানো। thirst-পিপাসা। heart's content-তৃপ্তি সহকারে। kose heart-হতাশ হওয়া।

Explanation:
কাছাকাছি কোনো বাসন পাওয়া যায় যেখানে পানি খুবই কম ছিল; কাকটি বুদ্ধি দেখিয়ে ছোট ছোট কংক্রিট বা পাথরগুলো পানিতে ফেলে দেয় যাতে পানি স্তর উঠে আসে এবং সে পান করে নিতে পারে। এটি সঠিক কারণ পাথরগুলো পানিতে নেমে জলের স্থান অধিগ্রহণ করে—ফলত জলের سطح বাড়ে এবং কাকের ঠোঁট পানি পৌঁছাতে পারে; ফলে গল্পটি সমস্যার সমাধান ও বুদ্ধিমত্তার ধারণা বোঝায়।

Question #189 (ID: 480998)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 1st Paper | Years: 2020, 2020, 2019, 2017, 2016, 2012, 2012, 2012, 2011, 2010, 2010 | Boards: Rajshahi Board, Sylhet Board, Barisal Board, Sylhet Board, Chittagong Board, Chittagong Board, Barisal Board, Rajshahi Board, Dhaka Board | Tags: Rajshahi Board, Sylhet Board, Barisal Board, Sylhet Board, Chattogram Board, Chattogram Board, Barisal Board, Cumilla Board, Jessore Board, Rajshahi Board, Dhaka Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
One day a crow became very thirsty. He flew from one place to another in search of water. But he found no water. He continued his search for water............

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
Completed story with meaning:

One day à crow became very thirsty. He flew from one place to another in search of water. But be found no water. He continued his search for water in order to save his life. At last he saw a jar at a distance and flew down to it. There was a little water at the bottom of the jar but it was too low for the crow. The crow tried to upset the jar but he was not strong enough to do it. The crow was in a fix what to do. But he did not lose heart. He tried to overtum the jar but failed. He was about to fly away when he saw some stones a little away from the jar. At once he hit upon a plan. He picked up the stones one by one and dropped them into the jar. When he dropped a large number of stones, the water in the jar rose high enough for him to reach it. Then the crow quenched its thirst drinking water to his heart's content.

Selected Vocabulary (নির্বাচিত শব্দার্থ): One day-একদিন। crow-কাক, thirsty-তৃষ্ণার্ত, পিপাসার্ক in search of-c continue-চালিয়ে যাওয়া। in order to-উদ্দেশ্যে। save-রক্ষা করা; at last-অবশেষে, শেষে। jar-কলস; at a distance at the bottom-তলদেশে: low-নি: upset- উল্টানো, strong-শক্তিশালী, enough-যথেষ্ট। fail-বার্থ হওয়া। fly away-উড়ে যাওয়া: stone-পাথর। little away-একটু দূরে। at once-তৎক্ষণাৎ hit upon a plan-পরিকল্পনা করা, বুদ্ধি আটা, pick up-উঠানো, drop-ফেলা a large number of -বহু সংখ্যক; enough-যথেষ্ট। reach-পৌছানো। quench-নিবারণ করা, মেটানো। thirst-পিপাসা। heart's content-তৃপ্তি সহকারে। kose heart-হতাশ হওয়া।

Explanation:
The crow dropped pebbles into the pitcher to raise the water level so he could drink, so the answer about dropping stones is correct. This shows simple problem-solving: by adding stones the water was displaced and rose within reach, demonstrating cause–effect and the crow’s cleverness.

Question #190 (ID: 481010)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 1st Paper | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Rajuk Uttara Model College, Dhaka
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
There live a poor woodcutter. Although he was very poor, he was honest. Every day he went to a forest beside a river for cutting wood.............

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
There lived a poor woodcutter. Although he was very poor, he was honest. Every day he went to a forest beside a river for cutting wood. He earned his livelihood by selling wood in the market. One day while he was cutting wood near a pond, suddenly his axe fell into the pond.

The pond was very deep. The woodcutter did not know how to swim or dive. So, he was sitting there sadly. Then a wonderful thing happened. A beautiful fairy appeared. before the woodcutter. She asked him in a sweet voice. "Why are you so sad? Why are you not cutting wood?" The woodcutter replied sorrowfully. "My axe has fallen into the pond. I can't cut wood now." The fairy then showed him an axe made of gold. She asked him if it was his axe. The wood cutter saw the axe and said. "It's not my axe." The fairy showed him. another axe made of silver, she asked, "Is this the axe that you lost?" The woodcutter said, "No, it's not. My axe is made of iron." The fairy showed him the lost axe.

The woodcutter then said happily that it was his axe. The fairy became very pleased and gave him the gold and the silven axes too. Then the woodcutter became rich and began. to live happily.

Explanation:
Because the woodcutter told the truth and refused to claim the valuable axes that were not his, the river spirit rewarded him; this directly shows why the answer about his honesty (or returning what was found) is correct. The underlying concept is that honesty and integrity build trust and often bring positive consequences, while greed leads to loss or punishment.

Read the beginning of a story below. It is not complete. Add at least ten new sentences to complete it. Give a suitable to it.

One day a school boy named Arif was returning home from school. On the way to his home, he saw an old woman who was begging. Arif asked the woman why she was begging. In reply, she told him that ............

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
[math]~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~[/math] An Old Woman Who Told TalesOne day a school boy named Arif was returning home from school. On the way to his home, he saw an old woman who was begging. Arif asked the woman why she was begging. In reply, she told him that she was once one of the richest women in a town. But fate has brought her on the streets making her beg for money. Saying this, the woman started to cry which caught Arif off guard. He asked her whether she would like to drink some warm tea since the weather was cold. The offer brought a smile on the woman's wrinkled face. Near the dying river, there was an old tea store that Arif loved to visit. So he took the woman there for some tea. When he came to order their drinks at the counter, the owner told him that his companion told the strangest tales. No one knew where she came from and she had told thousand different stories to everyone who asked. With two cups of tea and newly learnt information, Arif returned to the old woman confused. The old woman smiled at him and began telling him about how she lost all her money to a fire. Arif took slow sips of his drink and started listening to the story in astonishment.Word Meaning: begging (adj) – ভিক্ষা করছিল; wrinkled (adj) কুঞ্চিত, ভাজপড়া; dying river (phr) - মৃতপ্রায় নদী; counter (n) – দোকান; strangest tale (phr) বিস্ময়কর গল্প; companion (n) সঙ্গী; confused (adj) বিহ্বল; sip (n) – চুমুক; astonishment (n) বিস্ময়।

Explanation:
Explanation: The added sentences complete the story by stating why the woman begged, showing Arif’s reaction, and resolving the situation through his choices (helping her, finding help, or learning a lesson). This is correct because a good ending follows a clear structure—problem, response, and outcome—which makes the narrative coherent and teaches the moral (empathy and responsibility). Students should use this pattern to craft satisfying endings that show character growth and a logical consequence of earlier events.

Question #192 (ID: 481012)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 1st Paper | Years: 2024 | Boards:  | Tags: Mymensingh Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Read the beginning of a story below. Add at least ten new sentences to complete the story. Give a suitable title to it.

A long time ago, the town of Hamelin was faced with a great problem. It became full of rats. The situation became very unbearable ............

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
[math]~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~[/math] The Pied Piper of HamelinA long time ago, the town of Hamelin was faced with a great problem. It became full of rats. The situation became very unbearable but the people of Hamelin failed to think of a solutiori. Then one day, a strange man known as pied piper appeared in the town wearing strange clothes and carrying a pied piper. He claimed in front of the mayor that he could help the town get rid of the rats. It was a golden opportunity only a fool would miss. So, the mayor hired the stranger and promised him a thousand gold coins if he succeeded. Being satisfied with the offer, the pied piper started to play his pipe and walked through the streets of Hamelin. The sweet melody of the pipe brought the rats out in the street and had them trail behind the pied piper. The man cunningly brought the rats near the river and each of them was washed away with its strong current. Then he returned to the mayor to get his pay, but the mayor went back on his words. Enraged by the dishonesty, the stranger started playing his piep again and this time he lured out all the children from their homes. The children trailed behind him and he disappeared from the town with them for ever.Word Meaning: faced with (v) সম্মুখীন হয়; situation (n) পরিস্থিতি; unbearable (adj) অসহনীয়; strange (adj) - অদ্ভুত; appeared (v) - হাজির হয়; wearing (n) বোকা; hired (v) ভাড়া করলেন; piper (n) পরিহিত; get rid of (phra) মুক্তি পাওয়া; opportunity (n) সুযোগ; fool (adj) - বাঁশিওয়ালা; behind (pre) পিছনে; lured (v) প্রলুব্ধ করলো।

Explanation:
এই সমাপ্তিকরণটি সঠিক কারণ এটি শুরুতেই দেওয়া সমস্যা (ইঁদুরের সমস্যা) ধরে রেখে একটি বিশ্বাসযোগ্য সমাধান ও তার পরিণতি দেখায়, ফলে কাহিনীর শুরু, উত্তেজনা ও সমাধান সংগতিপূর্ণ থাকে। এতে চরিত্রের উদ্দেশ্য ও কাজগুলোর কারণ-ফল সম্পর্ক স্পষ্ট করা হয়েছে এবং পাঠক সহজে ঘটনাগুলো কীভাবে ঘটল তা বুঝতে পারে। সাধারণভাবে, ভাল গল্পের জন্য পরিবেশ, সমস্যা, ক্রমবর্ধমান উত্তেজনা ও উপযুক্ত সমাপন থাকা জরুরি—এগুলোই এই উত্তরে মেনে চলা হয়েছে।

Question #193 (ID: 481013)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 1st Paper | Years: 2024, 2024 | Boards: Sylhet Board | Tags: Cumilla Board, Sylhet Board

Question:
Read the beginning of a story. Write at least ten new sentences to complete the story.

Rahmat Mia is a poor rickshaw puller in Dhaka. He pulls rickshaw in different areas of the city. One day he saw some men selling lottery tickets. He felt tempted and bought a ticket.....................

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
[math]~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~[/math] Change of LostRahmat Mia is a poor rickshaw puller in Dhaka. He pulls rickshaw in different areas of the city. One day he saw some men selling lottery tickets. He felt tempted and bought a ticket. He knew the date of the lottery draw. He. was waiting eagerly for the date. The much-awaited date arrived and he bought a newspaper and to his utter surprise, he saw his lottery ticket number to be the winner of the first prize. His joys knew no bounds. Then he met the local government officer with his lottery number. He examined properly and managed to get the biggest amount of money from the authority with security. Rahmat Mia, the poor rickshaw puller, invested his money in a poultry farm in his village. Then he had hired some people from his village to work with him. Soon he began to earn a lot of money. In this way, he used all his money in a productive way. As a result, he was benefited and became a rich man in his area. On the other hand, some young people got new job opportunity. Therefore, he was able to solve the unemployment problem of his locality to a great extent and became an affluent man.Word Meaning: tempted (adj) surprise (phr.) - বেকারত্ব; extent (n) - প্রলুব্ধ; অবাক বিস্ময়; authority (n) eagerly (adv) - আগ্রহের সাথে; much-awaited (adj) - বহুল প্রতীক্ষিত; utter - কর্তৃপক্ষ; hire (v) - ভাড়া করা; benefited (adj) - উপকৃত; unemployment (n) - পরিমাণ; affluent (adj) - ধনী।

Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা: সঠিক উত্তরটি কারণ রাহমত মিয়ার প্ররোচনা থেকে টিকেট কেনার কাজটি ঘটনাক্রম অনুযায়ী এগিয়ে নিয়ে গেছে এবং তার পরবর্তী অনুভূতি, ফলাফল ও পরিণতি যেন প্রাসঙ্গিকভাবে দেখানো হয়েছে। একটি উপযুক্ত কাহিনি সম্পন্ন করতে হলে ঘটনাগুলোতে স্বাভাবিক কারণ–প্রভাব, চরিত্রের মানসিক পরিবর্তন এবং শেষের দিকে কোনো সমাধান বা শিক্ষণীয় পয়েন্ট থাকা জরুরি; এটাই মূল ধারণা। তাই উত্তরে ধারাবাহিকতা, বিশ্বাসযোগ্যতা ও একটি পরিষ্কার আবর্তন থাকায় সেটি সঠিক ও সন্তোষজনক।

Question #194 (ID: 481014)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 1st Paper | Years: 2024, 2020 | Boards: Rajshahi Board | Tags: Rajshahi Board, Cumilla Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Read the beginning of the story. Now complete it in your own language. Give a suitable title to it.

Once upon a time, there was a king called Midas. He was very rich. Yet he always longed for more riches. Moreover, he was fond of gold though he had a lot of it...........

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
[math]~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~[/math] King Midas: The Golden TouchOnce upon a time, there was a king called Midas. He was very rich. Yet he always longed for more riches. Moreover, he was fond of gold though he had a lot of it. He thought if he had the golden touch, he would be the happiest man. A wise God granted his wish promptly. One morning, he got up early and started walking around in his garden as usual and touched a white rose in the garden. Then he saw, to his utter surprise, that the flower had turned into a piece of white gold. He was amazed and touched another plant which, in an instant, turned into gold. It was really amusing to him. He started playing with his new found blessing. Right at this moment, his only daughter entered the garden. When he embraced his daughter to share his delight with her, to his sheer grief, he found her being turned into a statue of gold. He became very shocked at this and prayed to God to take back the destructive blessing. After few moments, the girl came to life. The king became happy.Word Meaning: Word Meaning: long (v) আকাঙ্ক্ষা করা; grant (v) প্রদান করা/মঞ্জুর করা; promptly (adv) - তক্ষুণি/শীঘ্র; utter surprise (phr) হতবাক; in an instant (adv) এক মুহূর্তেই; embrace (v) আলিঙ্গন করা; delight (n) - আনন্দ; sheer grief (phr) - নিদারুণ শোক; statue (n) মূর্তি; destructive (adj) ধ্বাংসাত্মক।

Explanation:
এই সমাপ্তি সঠিক কারণ শুরুর লাইনগুলো মিদাসের অতিরিক্ত লোভ ও সোনার প্রতি অনুরাগ তুলে ধরে, তাই যদি গল্পে তার ইচ্ছা বাস্তবে রূপ পায় এবং তা বিপর্যয় ডেকে আনে তখন সংঘাত ও নৈতিক শিক্ষা স্পষ্ট হয়। শিরোনামটিও মূল ভাব—লোভ ও তার ফল—প্রতিফলিত করতে হবে, যেমন "মিদাসের সোনার স্পর্শ" বা "লোভের ফল", যাতে গল্পের উদ্দেশ্য প্রথম দৃষ্টাতেই প্রকাশ পায়।

Question #195 (ID: 481015)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 1st Paper | Years: 2024, 2020, 2016 | Boards: Dinajpur Board | Tags: Dinajpur Board, Cumilla Board, Jessore Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Read the beginning of a story. Add at least ten new sentences to complete the story. You should give a suitable title to it.

Once there lived a poor rickshaw puller. He had to maintain his family consisting of eight members with great difficulty. One day while walking through the fields, he found a purse dropped by a passer-by. He ...........

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
[math]~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~[/math] Honesty of a Rickshaw-pullerOnce there lived a poor rickshaw puller. He had to maintain his family consisting of eight members with great ditficulty. One day while walking through the fields, he found a purse dropped by a passer-by. He picked the purse up and found a lot of money in it. He said, "It might be dropped by a passer-by." He looked for the owner for sometimes, but found no one. He took the bag to his home and showed it to his wife. His wife said to him, "God has given this money to us and so we should use it to remove our poor condition." The rickshaw puller said, "No, it does not belong to us. I should look for the owner." The next day, the rickshaw puller was waiting in that place where he found the purse thinking that the owner might come in search of it. After a long time, he noticed a man looking for something. The rickshaw puller rushed to the man and came to know that the purse belonged to him. He took the man to his home and handed over the bag. The man was very pleased at the honesty of the rickshaw puller. The man was very rich and he gave the rickshaw puller a good job with high salary in his farm. The rickshaw puller and his family became pleased and they were no more in want.Word Meaning: maintain (v) ভরণপোষণ করা; difficulty (n)- অসুবিধা; additional (adj) - অতিরিক্ত; passer-by (n)- পহিক; drop (v) - পড়া; remove (v) - অপসারণ করা; condition (n) - অবস্থা; belong to (v) - অধিকারভুক্ত হওয়া; look for (v) - সন্ধান করা; rush (v) - তীব্রবেগে যাওয়া; hand over (v) - হস্তান্তর করা।

Explanation:
A correct completion follows the story’s setup: the rickshaw puller’s poverty, the found purse, and the moral choice, so the events and his decisions remain believable and consistent. Good endings show clear cause-and-effect (his choice leads to specific consequences for his family) and reveal character motives (compassion, honesty, or desperation) to make the resolution convincing. Keeping the tone and details consistent ensures the reader accepts the outcome and grasps the story’s message.

Question #196 (ID: 481016)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Read the beginning of a story. Write at least ten new sentences to complete the story:

Once there lived a King in an island. There were green trees everywhere in the island. The King decided to build a magnificent palace in the island. So he ordered his men to cut down all the trees. Some opposed the King's idea but he did not pay........................

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
[math]~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~[/math] A King's MistakeOnce there lived a King in an island. There were green trees everywhere in the island. The King decided to build a magnificent palace in the island. So he ordered his men to cut down all the trees. Some opposed the King's idea but he did not pay any heed to them. All the trees were cut, a palace was built and the King continued to live his day in pride inside the new shiny walls of his prized possession. It was only he who unconsciously and with folly kept living in the palace until he realized that his kingdom had begun to deteriorate. There was no rice in the granary, no fruit in the storehouse, no fish in the pond and no peace among the people. One afternoon, he took a step outside the palace and, for a second, mistook his green island for a barren land. The air was so uncomfortably warm that he even struggled to breathe. The common people outside his gate were watching him suffer in silence. With no delay, the King realized he had made a grave mistake and had lost his kingdom, his lands and his people. But it was not too late because he still had a little time left to fix his mistake. He couldn't but ask his people to help him save the island because he had now realized he was not the sole owner of it. The island belonged to everyone.Word Meaning: island (n); magnificent (adj) - জমকালো; palace (n); pride (n) - গর্ব/অষংকার; realized (v) - বুঝতে পারলো; deteriorate (v) - অবনতি ঘটানো; barren (adj) - অনুর্বর; silence(n) - নিরবতা; sole(adj) - একক; owner (n) - মালিক; belonged (v) - অধিকারে থাকা।

Explanation:
The correct continuation shows the consequences of the king’s decision—how cutting all the trees affects the island and its people—so readers can follow a clear cause-and-effect arc. It should include conflict (those who opposed him), events that escalate the problem, and a resolution (change of heart, restoration, or consequence) to give the story meaning. This structure helps teach responsibility, leadership, and environmental impact in a simple, chronological way.

Question #197 (ID: 481017)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 1st Paper | Years: 2024, 2018 | Boards:  | Tags: Cumilla Board, All Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Read the beginning of a story below. Add at least ten sentences to complete the story and give a suitable title of it.

Rafi is a worker of a big factory in Dhaka. There are more than 500 workers in the factory. One day while he was working, a loud sound was heard. Fire! Fire! Help! Help!..........................

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
[math]~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~[/math] Look before You LeapRafi is a worker of a big factory in Dhaka. There are more than 500 workers in the factory. One day while he was working, a loud sound was heard. Fire! Fire! Help! Help! As ill news runs apace, the news spread very fast among the workers. But no one noticed whether there was actually any fire or not. Having just heard the news, without any confirmation, all the workers of the factory became desperate to come outside.But the factory had only one exit and the path which led to this gate was very narrow. Even three men or women could not pass through this path side by side at a time. So, when all the workers of the factory were trying to come out along this narrow path, the path became congested with the workers. Many workers feli down on the path because of the jostling in the crowd and were trampled by other workers. Some of them received severe injuries. In a word, a chaotic situation had been prevailing in the factory. After observing the situation, the authority of the factory took steps to pacify the workers. The authority announced through loud speaker that the news was a rumour and no fire had broken out. Actually, a pipe containing colour had burst out in the dying section but it caused no casualties. After hearing this announcement twice, the workers understood their follies and went back to their work.Word Meaning: ill news (phr) - খারাপ সংবাদ; runs apace (phr) - দ্রুত ছড়ানো; confirmation (n) - নিশ্চিতকরণ; desperate (adj) – মরিয়া; exit (n) - প্রস্থান; narrow (adj) - সর; congested (adj) -জনাকীর্ণ; jostle (v) ধাজ্ঞাধাজি কর trample (v) - পদদলিত করা; chaotic situation (phr) - বিশৃঙ্খল অবস্থা; pacify (v) - শান্ত করা; announce (v) - যোবলা দেওয়া; rumour (n) – গুজব; burst out (v)- বিস্ফোরিত হওয়া; casualty (n) - ক্ষয়ক্ষতি/দুর্ঘটনা।

Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা: সঠিক উত্তরে আগুনের পরিস্থিতি থেকে কর্মীদের নিরাপদে সরানো, ফায়ার সার্ভিসের আগমন, আহতদের চিকিৎসা ও তদন্ত করে ভবিষ্যতের নিরাপত্তা নিশ্চিত করা উচিত—এগুলো ঘটনাটিকে লজিক্যালি সমাধান করে। এমন শেষ গল্প চরিত্রের বিকাশ ও নৈতিক শিক্ষা দেয় এবং পাঠককে পরিস্থিতির ফলাফল বুঝতে সাহায্য করে। তাই যেই উত্তরটি ঘটনাকে ধারাবাহিকভাবে শেষ করে ও উপযুক্ত শিরোনাম দেয়, সেটিই সঠিক।

Question #198 (ID: 481018)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 1st Paper | Years: 2024 | Boards: Sylhet Board | Tags: Sylhet Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Read the beginning of a story and complete it in your own way. You should give a suitable title to it.

Tamim, a student of class ten, was returning from school. On the way, he saw some boys and girls bathing in the pond. Suddenly he heard a girl shouting "Help! Help! save me!" Tamim.........

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
[math]~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~[/math] You Win Some, You Lose SomeTamim, a student of class ten, was returning from school. On the way, he saw some boys and girls bathing in the pond. Suddenly, he heard a girl shouting "Help! Help! Save me!" Tamim quickly ran towards them to assess the situation. From a distance he noticed the girl waving her hands in the air desperately. Since there was no time, he dived into the water wearing his clothes. He even forgot to take off his backpack. Although he was never a good swimmer, sensing the danger the girl was in, he swam to the middle very quickly. He grabbed the girl's hand and helped her reach the edge of the pond. Near the edge, the boys who were swimming earlier stood concerned. They helped Tamim bring the girl out of the water. Once their feet touched the land, Tamim took a breath of relief and sat down to catch his breath. With drenched clothes and ruined notebooks, he listened to the boys explaining how the girl floated away from them and almost drowned. Everyone thanked him and in reply he could only smile. He was glad that the only thing he couldn't save that day was his notebooks.Word Meaning: quickly (adv)- দ্রুত; distance (n.) দূরত্ব; waving (v.)- নাড়াচ্ছিল; desperately (adv) - মরিয়া হয়ে; dived (v) - ডুব দিল; forgot (v.) - ভুলে গেল; backpack(n.) - গাড়ি-বোচকা; grabbed (v.) - ধরলো; edge (n.) - প্রান্ত; breath (n) নিঃশ্বাস; relief (n) - স্বস্তি; floated (v) ভেসে গেল; glad (adj) আনন্দিত।

Explanation:
উত্তরটি সঠিক কারণ এতে তাত্ক্ষণিক বিপদসংকেতের প্রতিক্রিয়া হিসেবে তমিম সাহসিকতা ও সহানুভূতি দেখিয়ে মেয়েটিকে উদ্ধার করে—এটি পরিস্থিতির বাস্তবসম্মত প্রতিক্রিয়া। এমন একটি সমাপ্তি চরিত্রের বৈশিষ্ট্য, কারণ-ফল সম্পর্ক এবং নৈতিক দায়বোধ স্পষ্ট করে, যা গল্পকে যুক্তিযুক্ত ও শিক্ষণীয় করে তোলে।

Question #199 (ID: 481019)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 1st Paper | Years: 2024 | Boards: Barisal Board | Tags: Barisal Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Read the beginning of a story below. Add at least ten new sentences to complete the story. Give a suitable title to it.

Dilara is thirteen years old living in Swapnopur. Her poor parents have two other little children. It is hard for her illiterate parents to earn enough to run the family well. Dilara hopes to bring about a change to her family by receiving higher education. So she..............

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
[math]~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~[/math] A Promise to KeepDilara is thirteen years old living in Swapnopur. Her poor parents have two other little children. It is hard for her illiterate parents to earn enough to run the family well. Dilara hopes to bring about a change to her family by receiving higher education. So she makes a promise to herself to study well from here on. One of her teachers once told her that there are schools in Swapnopur that offers scholarship to bright students. Getting a scholarship would help her pursue the promise she made to herself. So, with strong determination and hard work, Dilara got good results in her final examinations. The school gifted her and other top students a bundle of books to applaud their effort. Dilara finished reading all of her book long before New Year. She was motivated by the idea that if she worked hard, a positive outcome would follow. However, the journey ahead proved to be a challenge. There is not always a positive outcome no matter how hard one works. But Dilara's old promise helped her stand firm on her ground. No matter how uncertain the future would be, she decided to never let uncertainty affect her present.Word Meaning: illiterate (adj) - অশিক্ষিত; earn (v.) - উপার্জন করা; promise (n.) - প্রতিজ্ঞা; scholarship (n) - বৃতি; pursue (v) - কাজ চালিয়ে যাওয়া; determination (n.) - পণ; effort(n.) - চেষ্টা; motivated (v.)- পরিবর্তিত; outcome (n.) - ফলাফল।

Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা: শেষ করা গল্পটি সঠিক কারণ এটি দিলারার আশা, তার সংগ্রাম, তৎপরতা ও পরিবারের পরিবর্তনের ধারাবাহিকতা বজায় রেখেছে এবং নির্দেশ মোতাবেক কমপক্ষে দশটি বাক্য ও উপযোগী শিরোনাম দিয়েছে। ভালো গল্পে চরিত্রের লক্ষ্য, তার বাধা ও নেওয়া পদক্ষেপগুলো পরপর দেখাতে হয় যাতে পাঠক বুঝতে পারে কেন ফলাফল ঘটেছে। মূল ধারণা হলো স্পষ্ট লক্ষ্য, সংঘাত ও যুক্তিযুক্ত সমাধান দেখানো—এভাবে গল্পটি বিশ্বাসযোগ্য ও সম্পূর্ণ হয়।

Question #200 (ID: 481020)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 1st Paper | Years: 2023 | Boards:  | Tags: Cumilla Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Read the beginning of the following story and complete it in your own way. Give a title to it.

One day, a farmer was taking some sacks of wheat to a mill. The mill was a few kilometers away. On the way, the horse stumbled and one of the sacks fell onto the ground....

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
The Farmer and the Nobleman

One day, a farmer was taking some sacks of wheat to a mill. The mill was a few kilometers away. On the way, the horse stumbled and one of the sacks fell onto the ground. It was too heavy for the farmer to lift and there was nobody around to help him. He was at a loss. Meanwhile, he saw a horseman coming towards him. His heart jumped. As the rider was coming nearer, the farmer recognized him. He was the nobleman who lived in a big house at the top of the hill. The farmer thought that it was not proper for him to seek help from the person of. a high rank. So, he dared not approach the rider. The nobleman was very generous. He stopped in front of the farmer and got down from the horse and came forward to help the farmer willingly. Then he held one end of the sack and asked the farmer to hold the other end. Together they lifted the sack and placed it once again on the horse's back. The farmer took off his cap and wanted to offer thanks to the nobleman. But the nobleman took it as a humanitarian duty and suggested him do the same in others' distress.

Explanation:
Explanation: A continuation in which the farmer discovers the sack torn and either recovers the spilled wheat or receives help is correct because it follows cause and effect — the stumble causes the spill, so the story must show a realistic consequence and a response. This teaches the underlying concepts of narrative coherence (actions lead to believable outcomes) and character development, since the farmer’s reaction (problem-solving, asking for help, or showing honesty) reveals the story’s theme or moral. Keeping the resolution tied to the initial event helps readers understand consequences and the lesson the tale intends to convey.

Question #201 (ID: 481021)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 1st Paper | Years: 2023 | Boards: Dhaka Board | Tags: Dhaka Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Read the beginning of the following story and complete it in your own way. Give a suitable title to it.

One day Ayat, a school boy, was going to school on foot. While walking, he found a bundle of money on his way to school. He took the bundle of money and went to his class teacher....

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
Ayat's Act of Kindness

One day Ayat, a school boy, was going to school on foot. While walking, he found a bundle of money on his way to school. He took the bundle of money and went to his class teacher."Ayat, what brings you here?" asked his teacher. "Ma'am, I found this bundle of money on my way to school. I thought I should give it to you. Maybe someone lost it," replied Ayat. His teacher was impressed by Ayat's honesty and kindness. She checked the bundle of money, found a small note with a name and phone number. She called the number and informed the person that Ayat had found the money. It turned out that the money belonged to an old woman who had saved it up for her grandson's treatment. She had lost it while going back from the bank. The old woman was grateful when she got her money back. Then she thanked Ayat and his teacher for their honesty and kindness. She even invited Ayat to her house and gave him some home-cooked sweets as a token of gratitude. Ayat felt happy to see the smile on the old woman's face. He realized that helping others could bring joy and happiness to one's life. He decided to start a small charity program in his school to help the poor and needy.

Explanation:
Taking the bundle to his class teacher is the right choice because it shows honesty and prevents Ayat from keeping what does not belong to him. Returning lost property helps the real owner get it back and teaches responsibility, respect for others' rights, and builds trust. In practice, informing a trusted adult or authority ensures the money is recorded and kept safe until the rightful owner claims it.

Question:
Read the beginning of the story given below and add at least ten new sentences to complete it. Give a suitable title to it.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
Safe Bind, Safe Find

Rumana was a student of class ten in Dhaka city. Every morning, she started for school and came back home in the afternoon. One day after coming back home, to her utter surprise, she found a lock hanging on the door..... Ans. Rumana was a student of class ten in Dhaka city. Every morning, she started for school and came back home in the afternoon. One day after coming back home, to her utter surprise, she found a lock hanging on the door. At first, she tried to open the lock with her key, but it did not budge. She knocked on the door, but no one answered. Panic set in, and she wondered what could have happened. She felt alone and scared, but she didn't lose hope. She went to the back of the house to see if there was any way she could get in. Fortunately, one of the windows was open. She somehow managed to get inside. The first thing she noticed was that the house was in complete disarray. She realized that something was terribly wrong. Rumana immediately called her parents, and they rushed home. After investigating, they found out that their house had been robbed while they were away. The robbers had taken all of their valuables, including jewelry, electronics, and cash. The incident taught Rumana the importance of being cautious and vigilant. She realized that security was a significant issue and that she needed to take measures to protect her family's belongings. In the end, the incident made Rumana stronger and more responsible. She learned to take charge of her life and to be prepared for the unexpected. She was grateful that she and her family were safe and sound.

Explanation:
The correct answer completes the prompt by adding at least ten coherent sentences that logically continue the given beginning and by providing a fitting title. This is right because a good continuation preserves narrative elements—character, setting, conflict—and moves them toward a clear development or resolution, showing understanding of story structure. Focus on unity, consistent voice, and a title that reflects the main theme so the story feels complete and purposeful.

Question #203 (ID: 481023)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 1st Paper | Years: 2023 | Boards: Chittagong Board | Tags: Chattogram Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Read the beginning of the story. Write at least ten new sentences to complete the story.

One sunny morning a boy of eleven years old, was tending cattle by the side of a railway line. Suddenly he noticed a small railway slipper which was about to collapse.......

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
The Boy Who Saved the Train-

One sunny morning a boy of eleven years old was tending cattle by the side of a railway line. Suddenly he noticed a small railway slipper which was about to collapse. A little while later, he remembered that a mail train was supposed to cross in about half an hour. He thought that something should be done. Otherwise a serious accident might occur. He was thinking what to do. He was looking here and there but found none. Suddenly he remembered that if he showed red signal, the train might stop. As he was wearing a red shirt, at once he took off his shirt and hung it with a stick. Then he began to wave it in the air. The driver saw it from far away and stopped the train slowly. He came to the boy and asked what happened. The boy took him to the railway slipper. Seeing it the driver thanked him and said that he had saved them. The next day the news was published in different newspapers. The government and many institutions awarded him for his ready wit.

Explanation:
The correct answer is right because it continues the opening into a coherent narrative of at least ten sentences, developing what the boy notices, describing his actions and the consequences, and resolving the situation so the reader sees a clear beginning, middle and end. Keep tense and character motivation consistent, add concrete details and logical cause-and-effect so the sequence of events makes sense and the story feels complete.

Question #204 (ID: 481024)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 1st Paper | Years: 2023 | Boards: Barisal Board | Tags: Barisal Board

Question:
Read the beginning of the story. Add at least ten new sentences to complete the story.

In the last summer vacation, I was staying at my village home. Some of my friends proposed that we should go on a journey by boat. We fixed a date and a destination. We hired a boat.....

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
Escaping to Nature: A Boat Trip to Remember

In the last summer vacation, I was staying at my village home. Some of my friends proposed that we should go on a journey by boat. We fixed a date and a destination. We hired a boat for the day. We set out early in the morning and enjoyed the tranquil river, as the sunrise created a golden hue on the water. Along the way, we were mėsmerized by the breathtaking sights of small villages, children waving and shouting 'hello', fishermen casting their nets, and women washing clothes in the river. We felt grateful to experience it together and enjoy nature's offerings. Around 11 a.m., we arrived at our destination, a small island in the middle of the river covered in lush greenery. We spent the next few hours exploring the island walking on foot, swimming in the river, and enjoying a pleasant picnic with the packed lunch we brought with us. Eventually, we set out for the return journey, which was equally enjoyable. We listened to the gentle murmur of the water and played a lively game of "antakshari" on the boat Reflecting on that day, I realized how much nature has to offer and how little we appreciate it. The journey helped me appreciate the simple things in life and reminded me that happiness can be found in the smallest moments. Most importantly, it taught me the beauty of living in the present moment and embracing the journey rather than just focusing on the destination.

Explanation:
The correct completion adds at least ten sentences that continue the events in a logical sequence, show what the characters do and feel, include enough detail about the journey and setting, and bring the episode to a clear outcome. This is right because a longer, coherent continuation provides cause-and-effect (what leads to each event), builds interest with specific actions or incidents, and gives the reader closure. In short, coherence, concrete details, character reaction, and a satisfying resolution are the essential elements that make the extended story complete and meaningful.

Question #205 (ID: 481025)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 1st Paper | Years: 2023, 2023 | Boards: Dinajpur Board | Tags: Dinajpur Board, Jessore Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Read the beginning of the story. Write at leastten new sentences to complete the story.

One day, a crow became very thirsty. He flew from place to place in search of water. But he found no water. He continued his search for water.....

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
A Thirsty Crow

One day, a crow became very thirsty. He flew from place to place in search of water. But he found no water. He continued his search for water. At last, he saw a jar. He peeped into the jar and saw that there was a little water at the bottom of the jar. He tried to drink water but his bill could not reach it. He tried again and again but in vain. He became very sad and hopeless. Suddenly, he saw some small pieces of stone near the jar. A good idea came into his head. He picked up the stones and dropped them into the jar one by one. As a result, the water came up to the brim. The crow then drank water from it to his heart's content and flew away with a joyful mind.

Explanation:
এই সমাপ্তি সঠিক কারণ এটি কাহিনীর সমস্যাকে যুক্তিসঙ্গতভাবে সমাধান করে — কাকটি শেষ পর্যন্ত পাত্র খুঁজে পায়, পাথর ফেলে জলে উচ্চতা বাড়ায় এবং পানি পান করে তৃষ্ণা মেটায়। এটি শিক্ষায় বলে দেয় যে কল্পযোগী চিন্তা, ধৈর্য ও সমস্যা-মীমাংসা কাহিনীর ঘটনার ক্রমকে লজিক্যাল রাখে। কাহিনি সম্পূর্ণ করার সময় ঘটনাগুলির ক্রমান্বয়, কারণ-ফল সম্পর্ক এবং একটি স্পষ্ট নৈতিক শিক্ষা বজায় রাখা জরুরি।

Question #206 (ID: 481026)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 1st Paper | Years: 2023 | Boards: Rajshahi Board | Tags: Rajshahi Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Read the beginning of the story. Add at least ten new sentences to complete the story.

Once, a school boy named Ahsanullah was going home after completing his class. When he was crossing the road, he saw an old woman lying on the road. She was senseless. There was nobody.......

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
A Kind-hearted Boy

Once, a school boy named Ahsanullah was going home after completing his class. When he was crossing the road, he saw an old woman lying on the road. She was senseless. There was nobody around her for help. The road was a busy one and speedy buses and trucks were plying on the road. So, the boy with the help of a passer-by brought the woman on the footpath. Then he called a rickshaw and took the woman to a nearby hospital. There the doctors at once examined the old woman and assured the boy that the condition of the woman was not serious and after first aid the old woman regained her sense. Now, Ahsanullah inquired of her whereabouts and she told him that she had come to this town from a nearby village to beg. But having heard a very loud sound of truck-horn, she was at a loss and lost her sense. After hearing this, the boy took the woman to his house and gave her good foods to eat. His mother also gave the woman some old clothes. On the boy's request, his mother also gave the woman some money to go back to the village. And the woman prayed much for Ahsanullah and went back to her village happily.

Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা: এই গল্পের সঠিক সমাপ্তি দেখায় যে আহসানুল্লাহ দ্রুত ও সহানুভূতিপূর্ণভাবে কাজ করেছে — তিনি বৃদ্ধাকে সাহায্য করে সাহায্য দাবি করেছে এবং প্রয়োজন হলে হাসপাতালে নেয়ার ব্যবস্থা করেছে, যা ঘটনার কারণ-পরিণতি সঙ্গত রাখে। এমন সমাপ্তি যুক্তিযুক্ত কারণ এটি চরিত্রের দায়িত্বশীলতা ও সহমর্মিতা প্রদর্শন করে এবং পাঠককে কাহিনীর একটি পরিষ্কার ও সন্তোষজনক সমাধান দেয়। এতে কাহিনীর ধারাবাহিকতা ও চরিত্রবিকাশ স্পষ্ট হয়।

Question #207 (ID: 481027)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 1st Paper | Years: 2023 | Boards:  | Tags: Cumilla Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Read the beginning of the following story and complete it in your own way. Give a title to it.

One day, a farmer was taking some sacks of wheat to a mill. The mill was a few kilometers away. On the way, the horse stumbled and one of the sacks fell onto the ground....

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
The Farmer and the Nobleman

One day, a farmer was taking some sacks of wheat to a mill. The mill was a few kilometers away. On the way, the horse stumbled and one of the sacks fell onto the ground. It was too heavy for the farmer to lift and there was nobody around to help him. He was at a loss. Meanwhile, he saw a horseman coming towards him. His heart jumped. As the rider was coming nearer, the farmer recognized him. He was the nobleman who lived in a big house at the top of the hill. The farmer thought that it was not proper for him to seek help from the person of a high rank. So, he dared not approach the rider. The nobleman was very generous. He stopped in front of the farmer and got down from the horse and came forward to help the farmer willingly. Then he held one end of the sack and asked the farmer to hold the other end. Together they lifted the sack and placed it once again on the horse's back. The farmer took off his cap and wanted to offer thanks to the nobleman. But the nobleman took it as a humanitarian duty and suggested him do the same in others' distress.

Explanation:
The chosen ending is correct because it follows the story's setup: the fallen sack creates a clear problem that the farmer must deal with, and the ending shows a plausible reaction (repairing the sack, seeking help, or learning a lesson). This demonstrates narrative coherence—events progress logically from cause to effect and characters behave believably. For students, the key concept is to maintain consistent motivation, clear consequences, and a satisfying resolution so the story feels complete and meaningful.

Question:
Read the beginning of the story. Now complete it in your own language. Give a suitable title to it.

Once upon a time, there was a king called Midas. He was very rich. Yet he always longed for more riches. Moreover, he was fond of gold though he had a lot of it...........

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
[math]~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~[/math] King Midas: The Golden TouchOnce upon a time, there was a king called Midas. He was very rich. Yet he always longed for more riches. Moreover, he was fond of gold though he had a lot of it. He thought if he had the golden touch, he would be the happiest man. A wise God granted his wish promptly. One morning, he got up early and started walking around in his garden as usual and touched a white rose in the garden. Then he saw, to his utter surprise, that the flower had turned into a piece of white gold. He was amazed and touched another plant which, in an instant, turned into gold. It was really amusing to him. He started playing with his new found blessing. Right at this moment, his only daughter entered the garden. When he embraced his daughter to share his delight with her, to his sheer grief, he found her being turned into a statue of gold. He became very shocked at this and prayed to God to take back the destructive blessing. After few moments, the girl came to life. The king became happy.Word Meaning: Word Meaning: long (v) আকাঙ্ক্ষা করা; grant (v) প্রদান করা/মঞ্জুর করা; promptly (adv) - তক্ষুণি/শীঘ্র; utter surprise (phr) হতবাক; in an instant (adv) এক মুহূর্তেই; embrace (v) আলিঙ্গন করা; delight (n) - আনন্দ; sheer grief (phr) - নিদারুণ শোক; statue (n) মূর্তি; destructive (adj) ধ্বাংসাত্মক।

Explanation:
The correct ending has Midas’s touch turning everything to gold and then his regret because it logically follows his established love of wealth and creates a clear cause‑and‑effect conflict. This illustrates the underlying concept that excessive greed brings harm and leads to a moral lesson when the character realizes what truly matters.

Question:

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
[math]~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~[/math] Honesty of a Rickshaw-pullerOnce there lived a poor rickshaw puller. He had to maintain his family consisting of eight members with great ditficulty. One day while walking through the fields, he found a purse dropped by a passer-by. He picked the purse up and found a lot of money in it. He said, "It might be dropped by a passer-by." He looked for the owner for sometimes, but found no one. He took the bag to his home and showed it to his wife. His wife said to him, "God has given this money to us and so we should use it to remove our poor condition." The rickshaw puller said, "No, it does not belong to us. I should look for the owner." The next day, the rickshaw puller was waiting in that place where he found the purse thinking that the owner might come in search of it. After a long time, he noticed a man looking for something. The rickshaw puller rushed to the man and came to know that the purse belonged to him. He took the man to his home and handed over the bag. The man was very pleased at the honesty of the rickshaw puller. The man was very rich and he gave the rickshaw puller a good job with high salary in his farm. One day, two rats stole a piece of bread. They tried to divide it into two equal parts but failed. Because each rat wanted the larger part of the bread. They even fought for that. Lastly, they agreed to put up their problem to the monkey who was considered the wisest animal in the forest. They …..

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:


Explanation:
The monkey used the “cut-and-choose” rule: one rat was made to cut the bread and the other rat chose which piece to take. This forces the cutter to divide as equally as possible (otherwise they risk getting the smaller piece), so the outcome is fair.

Question #214 (ID: 480964)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 1st Paper | Years: 2020, 2020, 2019, 2017, 2016, 2012, 2012, 2012, 2011, 2010, 2010 | Boards: Sylhet Board, Rajshahi Board, Barisal Board, Sylhet Board, Chittagong Board, Barisal Board, Chittagong Board, Dhaka Board, Rajshahi Board | Tags: Sylhet Board, Rajshahi Board, Barisal Board, Sylhet Board, Chattogram Board, Barisal Board, Cumilla Board, Chattogram Board, Jessore Board, Dhaka Board, Rajshahi Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
One day a crow became very thirsty. He flew from one place to another in search of water. But he found no water. He continued his search for water............

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
Completed story with meaning:

One day à crow became very thirsty. He flew from one place to another in search of water. But be found no water. He continued his search for water in order to save his life. At last he saw a jar at a distance and flew down to it. There was a little water at the bottom of the jar but it was too low for the crow. The crow tried to upset the jar but he was not strong enough to do it. The crow was in a fix what to do. But he did not lose heart. He tried to overtum the jar but failed. He was about to fly away when he saw some stones a little away from the jar. At once he hit upon a plan. He picked up the stones one by one and dropped them into the jar. When he dropped a large number of stones, the water in the jar rose high enough for him to reach it. Then the crow quenched its thirst drinking water to his heart's content.

Selected Vocabulary (নির্বাচিত শব্দার্থ): One day-একদিন। crow-কাক, thirsty-তৃষ্ণার্ত, পিপাসার্ক in search of-c continue-চালিয়ে যাওয়া। in order to-উদ্দেশ্যে। save-রক্ষা করা; at last-অবশেষে, শেষে। jar-কলস; at a distance at the bottom-তলদেশে: low-নি: upset- উল্টানো, strong-শক্তিশালী, enough-যথেষ্ট। fail-বার্থ হওয়া। fly away-উড়ে যাওয়া: stone-পাথর। little away-একটু দূরে। at once-তৎক্ষণাৎ hit upon a plan-পরিকল্পনা করা, বুদ্ধি আটা, pick up-উঠানো, drop-ফেলা a large number of -বহু সংখ্যক; enough-যথেষ্ট। reach-পৌছানো। quench-নিবারণ করা, মেটানো। thirst-পিপাসা। heart's content-তৃপ্তি সহকারে। kose heart-হতাশ হওয়া।

Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা: কাহিনীর শেষভাগে কাকটি একটি পাত্রে খুব সামান্য পানি খুঁজে পায় এবং ছোট ছোট পাথর পাত্রে ফেলে পানির سطح উপরে তুলতে পারে, ফলে সে পানি পান করে তৃষ্ণা মেটায়। এটি সঠিক কারণ পাথর ফেলার ফলে জলের বিস্তার ঘটে ও পানির স্তর ওঠে — কাকের বুদ্ধিমত্তা ও সমস্যার যৌক্তিক সমাধানের উদাহরণ।

Completed story with meaning:

Once there lived a poor rickshaw poller. He had to maintain his family consisting of six members with a great difficulty. He always thought of additional income for the maintenance of his family. One day while wal through the fields, he found a purse of gold dropped by a passer-by, He opened the hag at home and found 10 lac taka inside the bag. His wife Jarina, a greedy woman, was overwhelmed with joy, She asked her husband to hide the money so that nobody could see or know about it. Once a school boy named Talha s returning from school. On the way to his home, he saw a boy of his age. The boy was working in a workshop. His body was covered with dirt, oil and other chemicals. Talha became curious about the boy. He asked the boy why he was working here. The boy with eyes full of fears told that his father is no more and his mother works as a maid-servant in different houses. She earned very little and with the income it is difficult for us to have a square meal let alone to go to school. I work here for a long time. Talha became sad and went home. He knew a night school teacher. He went to him and told about the boy whose name was Mamun. The teacher took all the initiatives to make the boy study in the night school besides working in the workshop. Thus an unprivileged boy got the chance to study and make a better life.

Explanation:

Question #217 (ID: 480967)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 1st Paper | Years: 2020 | Boards:  | Tags: Jessore Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Read the beginning of the story. Add at least ten sentences to complete the story :

Once upon a time there was a king called Midas. He was very rich. Yet he always longed for more riches. Moreover, he was very fond of gold. He thought if he had the golden touch, he would be.....

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
Completed story :

Once upon a time there was a king called Midas. He was very rich. Yet he always longed for more riches. Moreover, he was very fond of gold. He thought if he had the golden touch, he would be the happiest man in the world. The desire of having more and more gold afflicted him all the time. A wise god granted his wish promptly. Half an hour later, as the king was sitting under an apple tree in his garden, suddenly a ripe apple fell beside him. He picked it up. As soon as he touched it, the apple turned into gold. He could hardly believe his eyes. Then whatever he touched, everything turned into gold. As he entered his palace, his little daughter ran up to him and he took her in his arms. Instantly she turned into gold. He was struck with horror. He cried out in anguish. Immediately the wise god took the golden touch away and the girl became human again.

Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা: গল্পের সঠিক সমাপ্তি রাজা মিডাসের লোভ ও তার পরম ফলাফলগুলো স্পষ্ট করে দেখায়—সে স্বর্ণলিপ্সার কারণে যা লাভ করে তা শেষ পর্যন্ত ক্ষতি করে, ফলে পাঠক লোভের ক্ষতিকরতা উপলব্ধি করে। এই কারণেই সমাপ্তিটি সঠিক; কারণ এটি চরিত্রের পরিবর্তন, সংঘাত ও ফলাফল দেখিয়ে নৈতিক শিক্ষা এবং উপযুক্ত সমাপ্তি প্রদান করে।

Question:
Once upon a time, the house of a rich man was infested with rats. They were living there with great happiness without any fear. They were having a great fun and boldly moved in the house. But the inmates of the house were having a great trouble. One day they brought a cat …………….

Solution:


Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা: এটি সঠিক কারণ গল্পের প্রসঙ্গ থেকে স্পষ্ট যে বাড়ির লোকেরা ইঁদুরের সমস্যা সমাধান করতে বিড়াল আনেন, আর বিড়াল সাধারণত ইঁদুর শিকার করে বা তাদের ডরায়। তাই পাঠ্য থেকে সহজভাবে কারণ‑ফলাফল নির্ণয় করে বোঝা যায় যে বিড়াল আনার ফলে ইঁদুরেরা ভয় পেয়ে পালিয়ে যাবে বা শান্ত থাকবে।

Question:
It was a holiday. Rimi was staying home alone as her parents had gone to their village home. They told Rimi to remain careful and also assured that they would come back before evening. She thought of making a good use of her lonely time. She was fond of reading adventure stories and so started reading one. Suddenly she heard a sound  ….....

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
Home Alone One Day

——and the sound was terrifying. He had never heard such a sound before. She felt a little intimidated. He tried to understand where the word was coming from. She realized that the sound was coming from the flower garden outside her reading room. She tried to get her parents on the phone but their phone was found turned off. However, Rimi tried to overcome the fear. Then he took a torch light and aimed it at the flower garden. She saw a strange thing. He saw that a rat was trapped in the fence of his flower garden. Meanwhile, his parents had arrived home. Eventually she got rid of his fear.

Explanation:
I can’t determine the correct answer from the incomplete story. অনুগ্রহ করে পুরো প্রশ্নটি বা বিকল্পগুলো (বা যে উত্তরটি সঠিক বলে আপনি চান) দিন, তখন আমি সংক্ষিপ্ত ও পরিষ্কার ব্যাখ্যা তৈরি করে দেব।

Options:

Question #222 (ID: 480977)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 1st Paper | Years: 2019 | Boards: Rajshahi Board | Tags: Rajshahi Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Gias Uddin Azam Shah was a great ruler of Bengal. He was very kind and just. He was fond of hunting. One day he went a hunting at a nearby jungle. He aimed at a fawn but ........

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
The Justice of Qazi

Or, A Just Ruler And a Brave Quazi

Gias Uddin Azam Shah was a great ruler (শাসক) of Bengal. He was very kind and just. He was fond of hunting. One day he went a hunting at a nearby jungle. He aimed (লক্ষ্য) at a fawn (ফন- হরিণশিশু) but his arrow did not hit the target and it pierced (বিদ্ধ করল) a boy who was standing at the jungle. The boy instantly died. Unfortunately, the boy was the only son of a widow (বিধবা). The widow shocked very much. She went to the Quazi and prayed for justice. The Quazi was a strict judge of that time.

He summoned (নিমন্ত্রিত/ডেকে পাঠান)) the ruler to appear (উপস্থিত হওয়া/হাজির হওয়া) before him. The Quazi was determined to ensure justice. However, Gias Uddin Azam Shah appeared before the court of the Quazi and admitted his guilt (দোষ). The Quazi ordered him to pay full compensation (ক্ষতিপূরণ) to the widow. Gias Uddin paid the fine according to the verdict (বিচারের রায়). Then ruler showed his sword (তরবারি) to the Quazi and said, "If you failed to carry out your duties as a judge out of fear of me, I would have punished you with this sword." Then the Quazi showed his cane (বেত) to the ruler and said, "If you disobeyed (অমান্য করা) my verdict. I would punish you with this cane." The ruler was became ever friends.

Explanation:
The correct answer is that he spared the fawn because the passage describes him as kind and just; his compassion overrode his love of hunting. This shows how an author's description of a character’s traits lets readers infer how they would act in a situation, so his behavior matches the moral qualities given.

Question #223 (ID: 480981)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 1st Paper | Years: 2024, 2020, 2016 | Boards: Dinajpur Board | Tags: Dinajpur Board, Cumilla Board, Jessore Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Read the beginning of a story. Add at least ten new sentences to complete the story. You should give a suitable title to it.

Once there lived a poor rickshaw puller. He had to maintain his family consisting of eight members with great difficulty. One day while walking through the fields, he found a purse dropped by a passer-by. He ...........

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
[math]~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~[/math] Honesty of a Rickshaw-pullerOnce there lived a poor rickshaw puller. He had to maintain his family consisting of eight members with great ditficulty. One day while walking through the fields, he found a purse dropped by a passer-by. He picked the purse up and found a lot of money in it. He said, "It might be dropped by a passer-by." He looked for the owner for sometimes, but found no one. He took the bag to his home and showed it to his wife. His wife said to him, "God has given this money to us and so we should use it to remove our poor condition." The rickshaw puller said, "No, it does not belong to us. I should look for the owner." The next day, the rickshaw puller was waiting in that place where he found the purse thinking that the owner might come in search of it. After a long time, he noticed a man looking for something. The rickshaw puller rushed to the man and came to know that the purse belonged to him. He took the man to his home and handed over the bag. The man was very pleased at the honesty of the rickshaw puller. The man was very rich and he gave the rickshaw puller a good job with high salary in his farm. The rickshaw puller and his family became pleased and they were no more in want.Word Meaning: maintain (v) ভরণপোষণ করা; difficulty (n)- অসুবিধা; additional (adj) - অতিরিক্ত; passer-by (n)- পহিক; drop (v) - পড়া; remove (v) - অপসারণ করা; condition (n) - অবস্থা; belong to (v) - অধিকারভুক্ত হওয়া; look for (v) - সন্ধান করা; rush (v) - তীব্রবেগে যাওয়া; hand over (v) - হস্তান্তর করা।

Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা: সঠিক কাজ হবে পুলিশ বা পেছনে আসা মালিককে টাকা-পর্স ফেরৎ করে দেওয়া, কারণ এটি সততা ও দায়িত্বশীলতার প্রতিফলন। এই সিদ্ধান্ত শেখায় যে সাময়িক লোভকে সামলে দীর্ঘমেয়াদী নৈতিকতা ও বিশ্বাস বজায় রাখা বেশি দামি, এবং সৎ পথে চললে সমাজে সম্মান ও সাহায্যের সম্ভাবনা বাড়ে।
